                                       9              *
                                      10              *     13-April-1995  M. Durket
                                      11              *
                                      12              *     Changed the message: '<userid> is not accepting mail, mail not
                                      13              *     sent', to 'Mail not sent because mail is not being accepted
                                      14              *     by <userid>'. The reason is that in such messages, the
                                      15              *     <userid> portion is concatenated with the SET MAIL 'message'
                                      16              *     field (via an ACALL SEGMID), resulting in some weird looking
                                      17              *     messages like: 'Prism general access <HQ.PRM> -- Please
                                      18              *     respond to originator is not accepting mail, mail not sent.'
                                      19              *
